[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identification[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is a classic buffer size mismatch in the `%e/%E` format specifier[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandler in `src/fmt.c`:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m**: Allocates only [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes: `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m**: Tells `mg_dtoa` it has [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m bytes available: `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m326[0m[39m**: Calls `[0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which has no size parameter [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand can write up to [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m characters for large exponents[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is inconsistent with the correct pattern used for other format specifiers [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m%d/%u/%x/%g/%f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Allocate [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes at line [0m[1;36m275[0m[39m: `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Use `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m280[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, v, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pr, c == [0m[32m'g'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Fix Strategy[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix must be applied to `[0m[35m/src/mongoose/src/[0m[95mfmt.c[0m[39m` in the `mg_vxprintf` function,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically in the `%e/%E` format specifier handler [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m317[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Increase Buffer Size[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange line [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m from:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchar tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**: [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This matches the buffer size used for all other numeric format specifiers [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m%d/%u/%x/%g/%f[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at line [0m[1;36m275[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes is sufficient to handle:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Mantissa representation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mup to ~[0m[1;36m15[0m[39m significant digits for double precision[0m[1;39m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Null terminator[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Sign character[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Decimal point[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Any rounding artifacts from `mg_dtoa`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `mg_lld` function can write up to [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m characters for a [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-bit signed integer, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mso [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes provides adequate margin[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Use `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for Consistent Size Checking[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m from:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mk = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mk = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This ensures the size parameter passed to `mg_dtoa` matches the actual buffer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Follows the established pattern at line [0m[1;36m280[0m[39m: `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, v, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpr, c == [0m[32m'g'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Makes the code more maintainable - if buffer size changes, the call automatically[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madjusts[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Eliminates the hardcoded size mismatch that caused the overflow[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Verify No Additional Changes Needed[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLines [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m326[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m do not need modification because:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m**: `[0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout, param, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - The `k` value returned from `mg_dtoa` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill now be within bounds of the [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m326[0m[39m**: `[0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, exponent, [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - Will safely write to the [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmax [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m characters[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Line [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m**: `[0m[1;35mscpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout, param, tmp, k[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` - The `k` value from `mg_lld` will be [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change**: Only two lines need modification, reducing risk of [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintroducing new bugs[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Established Patterns**: Uses the same approach as the working %g/%f [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandlers[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves Functionality**: The fix doesn't change the logic or output format, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39monly the buffer safety[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Maintains Test Compatibility**: The existing unit tests at [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`test/unit_test.[0m[1;92mc:3654[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3662[0m[39m` will continue to pass[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **No Algorithmic Changes**: The mantissa/exponent calculation logic remains [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Same Output Format**: The scientific notation format [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmantissa + [0m[32m'e'[0m[35m/[0m[32m'E'[0m[39m + [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexponent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is preserved[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Same Function Calls**: Uses the same `mg_dtoa`, `mg_lld`, and `scpy` functions[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Backward Compatible**: External APIs and behavior remain identical[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issue[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates Buffer Overflow**: The [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer prevents the [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte overflow [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected by AddressSanitizer[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fixes Size Mismatch**: Using `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ensures `mg_dtoa` knows the true [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer size[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Handles All Cases**: Sufficient space for large exponents that `mg_lld` might [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgenerate[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Prevents Stack Corruption**: No more writing beyond stack frame boundaries[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Stack Usage Increase**: [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Impact: Each call to `mg_vxprintf` with %e/%E will use [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m additional bytes of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m40[0m[39m vs [0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: This is negligible and matches the stack usage of %g/%f format [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandlers already in production[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The codebase already allocates [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffers for similar operations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m275[0m[39m, line [0m[1;36m139[0m[39m in mg_dtoa[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **No Performance Impact**: [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stack allocation is extremely fast[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The actual formatting work [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfloating-point operations, string conversions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdominates execution time[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - External API unchanged[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Output format unchanged[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing tests continue to pass[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix directly mirrors the existing implementation pattern:[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Reference Implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m272[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m280[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'd'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'x'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'X'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'p'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'g'[0m[39m || c == [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'f'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    bool s = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'd'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, h = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'x'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'X'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'p'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m <-- [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    size_t xl = x ? [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'g'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'f'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        double v = [0m[1;35mva_arg[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*ap, double[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpr == ~0U[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pr = [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, v, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pr, c == [0m[32m'g'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m <-- [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m rest of handling [0m[33m...[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe %e/%E handler should follow this exact same pattern, which this fix [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccomplishes.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Implementation Notes[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Apply to Initial Codebase**: This patch must be applied to the initial source [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode at `[0m[35m/src/mongoose/src/[0m[95mfmt.c[0m[39m`[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line Numbers**: Target lines [0m[1;36m318[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m in the `mg_vxprintf` function[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Testing**: The existing unit tests at `test/unit_test.[0m[1;92mc:3654[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3662[0m[39m` should pass[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mafter this fix[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Verification**: The fuzzer should no longer trigger the stack-buffer-overflow [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith this patch applied[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` to `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Navigate to line [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m lines below[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` to `k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Save the file[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Open mongoose.c**[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Navigate to line [0m[1;36m820[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39minside the `[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mc == [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m || c == [0m[32m'E'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` block[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` to `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Navigate to line [0m[1;36m824[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m lines below[0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` to `k = [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, mantissa, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, c == [0m[32m'e'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Save the file[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why this is the optimal approach:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Follows Established Patterns**: This fix makes the [0m[32m'e'[0m[35m/[0m[32m'E'[0m[39m format specifier [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcase identical in structure to the [0m[32m'g'[0m[35m/[0m[32m'f'[0m[39m format specifier case [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/fmt.c lines [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m275[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m280[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which already correctly uses:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `char tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` for buffer allocation[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` for the function call[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Buffer Size Rationale**: The [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte size is not arbitrary:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `mg_dtoa` uses an internal buffer of [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39msrc/fmt.c line [0m[1;36m139[0m[39m: `char [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuf[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Floating-point formatting can produce lengthy strings [0m[1;39m([0m[39msign + digits + decimal[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpoint + precision digits[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte size provides sufficient space for all valid outputs from [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_dtoa`[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This size is already validated throughout the codebase[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Type Safety**: Using `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of a hardcoded value:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensures the size parameter always matches the actual buffer size[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Prevents future bugs if the buffer size is ever modified[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Is a defensive programming practice recommended for all buffer operations[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Makes the code self-documenting[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal and Surgical Changes**: Only [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m lines total across [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m files need [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodification, minimizing:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Risk of introducing new bugs[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Code review complexity[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Testing surface area[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Merge conflict potential[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Behavioral Changes**: The fix only changes internal buffer handling:[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The output format remains identical[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The mantissa calculation is unchanged[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The exponent calculation is unchanged  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The output sequence [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmantissa + [0m[32m'e'[0m[35m/[0m[32m'E'[0m[39m + exponent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is unchanged[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All existing test cases will produce the same results[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How it Preserves Existing Codebase Logic[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Preserved Functionality:**[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Format Specifier Parsing**: The entire format string parsing logic in [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_vxprintf` remains unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m245[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m342[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Variable Argument Handling**: The `[0m[1;35mva_arg[0m[1;39m([0m[39m*ap, double[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call at line [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m821[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains unchanged[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Mantissa/Exponent Calculation**: The scientific notation calculation logic [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains identical:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `int64_t exponent = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint64_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mlog10[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mmy_fabs[0m[1;39m([0m[39md[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m320[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m822[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `double mantissa = d [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35mpower[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, exponent[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m321[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m823[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Output Sequence**: The three-part output remains unchanged:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mantissa formatting via `mg_dtoa` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m322[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m824[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Output mantissa via `scpy` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m825[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Output [0m[32m'e'[0m[39m or [0m[32m'E'[0m[39m character [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m826[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Format exponent via `mg_lld` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m326[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m828[0m[1;39m)[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Output exponent via `scpy` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m327[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m829[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Other Format Specifiers**: All other format specifiers [0m[1;39m([0m[32m'd'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'x'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'X'[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m'p'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'g'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'm'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'M'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'c'[0m[39m, [0m[32m's'[0m[39m, [0m[32m'%'[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are completely unaffected[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Function Interfaces**: No function signatures are modified:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar *dst, size_t dstlen, double d, int width, bool tz[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remains [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mmg_lld[0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar *buf, int64_t val, bool is_signed, bool is_hex[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remains [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mmg_vxprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remains unchanged[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How it Addresses the Issues in the Evaluation Report[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Eliminates the Stack-Buffer-Overflow:**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fixes Buffer Undersizing**: [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer provides ample space for any output from `mg_dtoa`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Even in worst-case scenarios [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvery long mantissa representations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the buffer [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwon't overflow[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The buffer is also used for exponent formatting via `mg_lld` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m326[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m828[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich needs at most ~[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m characters for a [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m-bit integer[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Fixes Size Parameter Mismatch**:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` evaluates to [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m, which exactly matches the actual buffer size[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `mg_dtoa` internally calls `[0m[1;35mmg_snprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdst, dstlen, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, buf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m204[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it creates an iobuf with correct size[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The iobuf structure will have `buf` pointing to a [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte buffer and `[0m[33msize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m40[0m[39m`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This prevents writes beyond the buffer boundary in `mg_pfn_iobuf_private`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Breaks the Vulnerability Chain**:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Before Fix:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   mg_vxprintf [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m317[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → allocates tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → calls [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Wrong size![0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → mg_dtoa calls [0m[1;35mmg_snprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → mg_vsnprintf creates iobuf[0m[1;39m{[0m[33mbuf[0m[39m=[0m[35mtmp[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[33msize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m10[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Mismatch![0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → mg_vxprintf [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrecursive[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → scpy → mg_putchar_iobuf_static[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → mg_pfn_iobuf_private checks [0m[32m"if [0m[32m([0m[32mio->len + 2 <= 10[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Allows write to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mposition [0m[1;36m9[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → OVERFLOW at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbeyond [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte boundary[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   After Fix:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   mg_vxprintf [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m317[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → allocates tmp[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m][0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → calls [0m[1;35mmg_dtoa[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m40[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → mg_dtoa calls [0m[1;35mmg_snprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtmp, [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → mg_vsnprintf creates iobuf[0m[1;39m{[0m[33mbuf[0m[39m=[0m[35mtmp[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m[33msize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m40[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Match![0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → mg_vxprintf [0m[1;39m([0m[39mrecursive[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → scpy → mg_putchar_iobuf_static[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → mg_pfn_iobuf_private checks [0m[32m"if [0m[32m([0m[32mio->len + 2 <= 40[0m[32m)[0m[32m"[0m[39m  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Safe writes[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     → NO OVERFLOW - all writes within [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m-byte boundary[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Matches AddressSanitizer Stack Frame Analysis**:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Before fix: Stack frame shows `tmp371` at offset [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m112[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m120[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - only [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m bytes[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After fix: The buffer will be [0m[1;36m40[0m[39m bytes, preventing overflow at offset [0m[1;36m120[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The stack frame will show a larger buffer at the same location, with no [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Addresses Why Previous Patch Failed[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe previous patch attempted to fix the issue but **modified the wrong code [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocation**:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimal[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
